	<script type="text/javascript">
	window.G = {"conf" : {"windowSize" : 0}};

	var viewport = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth,
		stage = document.getElementById('zaz-gambit'),
		reducePage = false;

	if (viewport < 1024) {
		stage.setAttribute('class', 'w768');
		window.G.conf.windowSize = 768;
	} else if (viewport < 1280) {
		if(reducePage === true){
			stage.setAttribute('class', 'w768');
			window.G.conf.windowSize = 768;
		}else{
			stage.setAttribute('class', 'w1024');
			window.G.conf.windowSize = 1024;
		}
	} else if (viewport >= 1280) {
		if(reducePage === true){
			stage.setAttribute('class', 'w1024');
			window.G.conf.windowSize = 1024;
		}else{
			stage.setAttribute('class', 'w1280');

(function() {
    'use strict';
    if (!window.zaz || typeof window.zaz.use != 'function') {
        throw new Error('Framework not found as "window.zaz".');
    }
    window.zaz.use(function(pkg) {
        try {
            if (typeof pkg.includer != 'object') {
                throw new Error('Includer not delivered on this pkg');
            }
            if (includerComponents.length > 0) {
                pkg.includer.registerFetchedComponents(includerComponents[0].components);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            e.message = 'Error on Includer\'s reporter: ' + e.messsage;
            if (window.console && typeof window.console.error == 'function') {
                window.console.error(e);
            }
        }
    });

<div class="subheader">
<h1>Computer Science > Computers and Society</h1>
</div>
<h1 class="title mathjax"><span class="descriptor">Title:</span>
Breaking the News: First Impressions Matter on Online News</h1>
<div class="authors"><span class="descriptor">Authors:</span>
<a href="/find/cs/1/au:+Reis_J/0/1/0/all/0/1">Julio Reis</a>, 
<a href="/find/cs/1/au:+Benevenuto_F/0/1/0/all/0/1">Fabr&#x131;cio Benevenuto</a>, 
<a href="/find/cs/1/au:+Melo_P/0/1/0/all/0/1">Pedro O.S. Vaz de Melo</a>, 
<a href="/find/cs/1/au:+Prates_R/0/1/0/all/0/1">Raquel Prates</a>, 
<a href="/find/cs/1/au:+Kwak_H/0/1/0/all/0/1">Haewoon Kwak</a>, 
<a href="/find/cs/1/au:+An_J/0/1/0/all/0/1">Jisun An</a></div>
<div class="dateline">(Submitted on 26 Mar 2015 (<a href="/abs/1503.07921v1">v1</a>), last revised 16 Apr 2015 (this version, v2))</div>
<blockquote class="abstract mathjax">
<span class="descriptor">Abstract:</span> A growing number of people are changing the way they consume news, replacing
the traditional physical newspapers and magazines by their virtual online
versions or/and weblogs. The interactivity and immediacy present in online news
are changing the way news are being produced and exposed by media corporations.
News websites have to create effective strategies to catch people's attention
and attract their clicks. In this paper we investigate possible strategies used
by online news corporations in the design of their news headlines. We analyze
the content of 69,907 headlines produced by four major global media
corporations during a minimum of eight consecutive months in 2014. In order to
discover strategies that could be used to attract clicks, we extracted features
from the text of the news headlines related to the sentiment polarity of the
headline. We discovered that the sentiment of the headline is strongly related
to the popularity of the news and also with the dynamics of the posted comments
on that particular news.
</blockquote>

sx_310e67"></i></a></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="_5pbx userContent" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"><p>Análise do discurso</p><p> O Departamento de Letras e Literaturas Modernas da UFRN realiza, na quarta-feira, 29, uma nova edição do Projeto Me explica, me ensina, sobre análise do discurso. O encontro acontece no auditório B do CCHLA, a partir das 19h, e tem como convidados os professores  Orison Marden e Maria da Penha Casado. O projeto de periodicidade mensal é coordenado pela professora Izabel Nascimento e tem como proposta traçar um panorama dos estudos dialógicos voltados à literatura (em língua materna ou em língua estrangeira), enfatizando, em especial, os temas: o discurso no romance, a análise sociológica da literatura e a relação entre língua e literatura. As inscrições serão feitas no local do evento e serão emitidos certificados para os participantes.</p></div><div class="_3x-2"><div
